***onmacht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onmacht.html>onmacht</a> (80871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:on-.html>on-</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:macht.html>macht</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">usually uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">powerlessness</span>, the state of lacking power</li>

<p><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">powerlessness</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span>

<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bewusteloosheid.html>bewusteloosheid</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bezwijming</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***onmachtig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onmachtig.html>onmachtig</a> (56460)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">onmachtich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">unmahtig</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onmacht.html>onmacht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onmachtig.html>onmachtig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onmachtig.html>onmachtiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">onmachtigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">powerless</span>, lacking (sufficient) power</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">incapable</span>, lacking capability, knowledge or command</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">unconscious</span></li></ol>

***onrein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onrein.html>onrein</a> (26544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:onrein.html>onreine</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">unreini</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:on-.html>on-</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">rein</i>.
</p>

***ons.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> (73)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unsiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> (<i>personal</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>us (objective form of <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagelijks.html>dagelijks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Give <b>us</b> today our daily bread.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*unsa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*unseraz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></b>, <i>inflected form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>our <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">neuter</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heden.html>heden</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagelijks.html>dagelijks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brood.html>brood</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Give us <b>our</b> daily bread</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="NavFrame" style="float: left; width: 65em">
<div class="NavHead" style="background: CCCCFF;">Dutch personal pronouns</div>
<div class="NavContent">

</div></div>
<p><br clear="all" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Only used with singular neuter nouns in dependent clauses; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in all other situations as an independent possessive as well as with male and female nouns.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">unce</i> (1240), borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">uncia</i> (a twelfth of a pound) probably <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">once</i>. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ons.html>ons</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">onsen</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onzen.html>onzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onsje.html>onsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">metric ounce</span> (100 <span class="Latn" lang="en">grams</span>)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Prior to the law of 1820 that introduced the metric system in what then united both the Netherlands and Belgium a variety of measures ranging around ca 30 grams <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> known by this name. The law of 1820 attributed the name to the hectogram of 100 grams. In 1937 the IJkwet of the Netherlands officially abolished the term, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still commonly used.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hectogram</span></li></ul>
<div class="mw-references-wrap"><ol class="references">

</li>
</ol></div>

***ontaarden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontaarden.html>ontaarden</a> (44948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aarden.html>aarden</a></i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontaarden.html>ontaarden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to degenerate
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:feest.html>feest</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontaard.html>ontaard</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> braspartij.</i>
<dl><dd>The party <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> degenerated into an orgy of eating and drinking.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to corrupt</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ontbinding.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a> (18006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinden.html>ontbinden</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to decompose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbindingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Decomposition (e.g. of organic matter or in mathematics).
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kadaver.html>kadaver</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkeert.html>verkeert</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a>.</b>
<dl><dd><i>The cadaver <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> decomposing.</i></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 46 in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> priemfactoren <a href = vnd.unilang:geeft.html>geeft</a> 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> 23.</i>
<dl><dd><i>The decomposition of 46 into its underlying primes yields 2 and 23.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>Dissolution (e.g. of a legal entity).
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vereniging.html>vereniging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vond.html>vond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a> in 1931.</i>
<dl><dd><i>The dissolution of the society <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> place in 1931.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinding.html>ontbinding</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontbinden.html>ontbinden</a></li>

***ontbloten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontbloten.html>ontbloten</a> (48795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ont-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">de-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bloot.html>bloot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bare, naked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

</p><p><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>To bare, render naked</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To strip bare an object</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ontbloten.html>ontbloten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a></i>) To rid of, deprive of</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onterecht.html>onterecht</a> (12905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:on-.html>on-</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:terecht.html>terecht</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">unreasonable</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">unjust</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">unfair</span></li>
